### Excluded Patterns

The following are automatically excluded:

- `node_modules`
- `dist`
- `build`
- `.git`
- `coverage`
- `.next`
- `out`
- `__tests__`
- `vendor`
- `backup`
- `__pycache__`
- `target`
- `.venv`
- `venv`
- `tmp`
- `temp`
- `.cache`
- Hidden files and directories (starting with `.`)
